RISK FACTORS 
1. RISKS DERIVING FROM THE LEGAL STATUS AND BUSINESS OF THE 
FUND 
1.1. 
Nature of the Fund and obligations of the Sociedad Gestora  
The Fund will constitute a separate fund without legal status that, pursuant to Royal Decree 
926/1998, will be serviced by a management company (hereinafter "Sociedad Gestora"). The Fund 
will only be liable for its obligations vis-à-vis its creditors with its assets. 
The Sociedad Gestora will perform for the Fund those duties attributed to it in Royal Decree 
926/1998, as well as safeguarding the interests of the Security holders as the manager of third 
party funds, without there being any syndicate of Security holders. Therefore the capacity to 
defend the Security holders' interests depends on the means and resources of the Sociedad Gestora. 
1.2. 
Mandatory substitution of the Sociedad Gestora 
In accordance with article 19 of Royal Decree 926/1998, if the Sociedad Gestora is declared 
insolvent, without prejudice to the effects of such insolvency as described below, it will find 
another sociedad gestora to substitute it. Whenever in the circumstances envisaged, four (4) 
months have elapsed since the event requiring the substitution occurs and a new sociedad gestora 
that is prepared to take over the management has not been found, the Fund will be liquidated early 
and the securities it has issued will be redeemed, in accordance with the provisions of the Articles 
of Incorporation and this Prospectus. 
1.3. 
Insolvency of the Sociedad Gestora 
The insolvency of any of the parties involved (whether it be either of the Sellers, the Sociedad 
Gestora or any other counterparty of the Fund) could affect their contractual relations with the 
Fund as provided in the Ley Concursal 22/2003 of 9 July (Spanish Insolvency Act - the “Ley 
Concursal”). 
In this respect, if the Sociedad Gestora is declared bankrupt, it must be substituted by another 
Sociedad Gestora in accordance with the provisions of the previous section of this Prospectus. 
Notwithstanding the foregoing, in the event of the insolvency of the Sociedad Gestora, any assets 
of the Fund that are in the possession of the Sociedad Gestora and with respect whereto the latter 
has no right of use, surety or retention -except for money due to its fungible nature- and that form 
part of the latter's assets will be construed as belonging to the Fund, and the receivers in 
bankruptcy must deliver them at the Fund's request. Due to the nature of the asset securitization 
operation in question, and except in the event of a breach by the parties, no cash amounts will 
become part of the assets of the Sociedad Gestora because the amounts that constitute the revenues 
of the Fund must be deposited, in the terms set forth in the Articles of Incorporation and in the 
Prospectus, in the accounts opened on behalf of the Fund by the Sociedad Gestora (which is 
involved in opening such accounts not only as the agent of the Fund, but as its legal representative.  
Therefore the Fund would be entitled to absolute separation in this respect, in the terms set forth in 
articles 80 and 81 of the Ley Concursal). 
In the event of the insolvency of an Seller, the issue and assignment of the respective 
Participations and Certificates may be returned only if an action for such return is pursued in

which fraud is demonstrated to have existed in that issue and assignment in accordance with the 
provisions of the paragraph 4 of the Fifth Additional Provision of Ley 3/1994. 
In the event that one of the Sellers is declared insolvent under the Ley Concursal, the Fund, acting 
through the Sociedad Gestora, will be entitled to separation with respect to the multiple securities 
representing the Participations and the Certificates that it has issued, in the terms set forth in 
articles 80 and 81 of the Ley Concursal. Furthermore the Fund, acting through its Sociedad 
Gestora, will be entitled to secure from the Seller in question the amounts derived from the 
Participations and the Certificates that it has issued, because such amounts will be construed as the 
property of the Fund and, therefore, must be transferred to the Sociedad Gestora on behalf of the 
Fund. Nevertheless, it might not be possible to exercise such separation right with respect to the 
funds handled by the Seller in question, for the account and pursuant to the orders of the Fund, in 
its duty of managing the collection of the Mortgage Loans that it services and the money on 
deposit, if any, in the Reinvestment Account opened by such Seller, in both cases as at the date the 
insolvency was declared, due to the fungible nature of money and the consequent confusion of 
assets. The mechanisms available for mitigating such risk are described in sections 3.4.4.3. 
(Reinvestment Accounts), 3.4.5. (How payments are collected in respect of the assets) and 3.7.1. 
(Servicing and custody of the Mortgage Loans) of the Additional Building Block. 
1.4. 
Restricted actions against the Sociedad Gestora 
The Security holders and remaining ordinary creditors of the Fund will have no recourse against 
the Sociedad Gestora, other than from non-performance of its duties or non-compliance with the 
provisions of the Articles of Incorporation and this Prospectus.   
2. RISK DERIVED FROM THE SECURITIES 
2.1. 
Liquidity 
There is no guarantee that a minimum volume or frequency of Security transactions will be 
forthcoming in the market. 
There is no commitment that any entity will intervene in the secondary market, providing liquidity 
to the Securities by offering itself as counterparty. 
Furthermore, under no circumstances will the Fund be able to repurchase the Securities from their 
holders, although the Bonds can be redeemed early in full in the case of early liquidation, under 
the terms established in section 4.4.3. of the Registration Document. 
2.2. 
Rate of Return of the Securities 
The calculation of the internal rate of return (IRR) for the holder of each Security that is stipulated 
in section 4.10. of the Securities Note, is subject, inter alia, to future market interest rates, given 
the floating nature of the Nominal Interest Rate of each Series, and to early redemption and default 
rate hypotheses that might not be fulfilled. 
2.3. 
Duration of the Securities 
The calculation of the average life of the Bonds of each Series and of the duration of the Securities 
mentioned in section 4.10. of the Securities Note is subject, inter alia, to Credit Right early 
redemption and default rate hypotheses that might not be fulfilled. Fulfilment of the early

Informativo" drafted in the Spanish language is the only official document, and no document other than the "Folleto Informativo"shall have

redemption rate is influenced by a variety of demographic, economic and social factors, such as 
seasonality, market interest rates, the employment and financial situation of the Mortgagors and 
the general state of the economy, that make this unpredictable. 
2.4. 
Default interest 
Under no circumstances will the delay of the payment of interest or repayment of principal to the 
Security holders give rise to accrual of default interest in their favour.  
3. RISKS DERIVED FROM THE ASSETS BACKING THE ISSUE 
3.1. 
Risk of default on the Mortgage Loans 
The Holders of the Securities issued by the Fund will bear the risk of default on the Mortgage 
Loans pooled in the Fund through the issue of the Participations and the Certificates, always taking 
into account the protection offered by the credit enhancement mechanisms referred to in section 
3.4.2. of the Additional Building Block. 
The Sellers, in accordance with article 348 of the Commercial Code, will only be held liable vis-à-
vis the Fund for the existence and legitimacy of the Mortgage Loans, and of the Participations and 
Certificates that they have issued, in the terms and conditions declared in the Articles of 
Incorporation and that are set forth in this Prospectus, as well as for the legal status with which 
they carry out the transfer. However, they will not assume any liability for the non-payment by the 
Mortgagors, be it of the principal, of the interest or any other amount they may owe by virtue of 
the Mortgage Loans. Nor will they assume, in any other form, liability for directly or indirectly 
guaranteeing the successful outcome of the transaction, nor will they grant guarantees or 
endorsements, nor will they be party to repurchase agreements relating to the Participations and 
the Certificates, either by virtue of the Articles of Incorporation, this Prospectus, or of any other 
agreement or contract. All of this, without prejudice to the Sellers being held liable for the 
replacement of the respective Participations and/or Certificates issued by each one that do not 
conform to the declarations set forth in section 2.2.8. of the Additional Building Block, in relation 
to the commitments given in sections 2.2.9 and 3.7.1. of the Additional Building Block. 
The Securities issued by the Fund do not represent or constitute an obligation of the Sellers or of 
the Sociedad Gestora. No other guarantees have been granted by any public or private entities, 
including the Sellers, the Sociedad Gestora, and any other firm affiliated with or invested in by any 
of the above. 
3.2. 
Limited protection 
An investment in the Securities may be affected, inter alia, by a worsening of the general 
economic conditions that have a negative effect on the payments of the Mortgage Loans that back 
the Fund issue. In the event that the level of Mortgage Loan default becomes high, the limited 
protection against Mortgage Loan portfolio loss afforded to the Securities as a result of the 
existence of the credit enhancement transactions described under section 3.4.2. of the Additional 
Building Block could be reduced, or even exhausted.  
Similarly, the degree of subordination of the Security interest payments and repayment of principal 
among the Bonds of the different Series that arises from their ranking in the Payment Priority 
Order constitutes a differentiated protection mechanism between the different Securities.

3.3. 
Risk of early redemption of the Mortgage Loans 
The Participations and the Certificates pooled in the Fund may be prepaid when the Mortgagors 
prepay the outstanding principal of the Mortgage Loans, in the terms set forth in each Mortgage 
Loan deed. Similarly, the Participations and the Certificates will be redeemed in full if that Seller 
is replaced in the related Mortgage Loans by another financial institution duly authorised for such 
purpose, subject to the Ley 2/1994 sobre subrogación y modificación de préstamos hipotecarios 
(Act 2/1994, of 30 March, on the subrogation and amendment of mortgages loans), in its current 
wording, or for any other reason having the same effect.  
The risk of such early redemption will be transferred on each Payment Date to the Security holders 
in accordance with the repayment rules set forth in section 4.9. of the Securities Note. 
Consequently, there may be changes in the repayment of the Bonds with respect to the amounts 
initially scheduled for each Payment Date.  
3.4. 
Seller NPL Ratios 
According to the financial information selected from section 3.5. of the Additional Building Block, 
as at 30 September 2005, the NPL Ratio is 0.63%, 1.17% and 3.75% for Caja Castilla La Mancha, 
Credifimo and Bankpime respectively, and the NPL Coverage Ratio is 321.39%, 82.32% and 
74.54% for Caja Castilla La Mancha, Credifimo and Bankpime respectively.

Fund Auditors

to appoint new statutory auditors of renowned prestige, notice would be given to the CNMV, the 
Rating Agencies and the Security holders, pursuant to the provisions of section 4.1.3 of the 
Additional Building Block.

2.2. 
Accounting principles used by the Fund 
The Fund will report income and expense in accordance with the accrual principle, that is, on the 
basis of the actual flows represented by those revenues and expenses, regardless of when they are 
collected and paid. 
a) Participations and Certificates subscribed by the Fund: the Participations and the Certificates 
have been recorded under the assets of the Fund at their face value, which is the same as their 
acquisition cost. 
The interest on the Participations and the Certificates is recorded in the income statement in 
accordance with the accrual principle. 
The due but unpaid interest on defaulted Mortgage Loan Participations and Certificates is recorded 
as an asset on the balance sheet. 
The interest due and the outstanding principal of the defaulted Mortgage Loan Participations and 
Certificates is recorded as an asset, except whenever it can be demonstrated that the mortgaged 
property is insufficient guarantee. 
b) Bonds issued: the Bonds are recorded as a liability on the Fund balance sheet, at an amount 
equal to their redemption value.  
The interest payable on the Bonds is recorded in the income statement on a cumulative basis, and 
the part of them that has been accumulated in line with the accrual principle that is due but remains 
unpaid is recorded in the related liabilities account. 
c) IO Securities: the subscription price of each security, adjusted from time to time by the IO 
Payments until such time, will be recorded as a liability of the Fund. 
d) Fund Accounts: Fund liquidity accounts maintained by the Paying Agent and, where applicable, 
by the Rated Sellers, with predefined reinvestment mechanisms. 
The balance of the accounts will be recorded as an asset of the Fund, while the income and 
expenses of such accounts form part of the income and expenses of the Fund. 
e) Operating expenses, fees and remuneration: all the fees and expenses are deductible in their 
accrual period. The Fund Incorporation and Securities Issue Expenses detailed in section 0. of the 
Securities Note will be written off by the straight-line method over twenty (20) consecutive 
Payment Dates, starting on 22 March 2006. 
e) Technical Advances: on each Calculation Date, the Technical Advance obtained on the previous 
Calculation Date is considered deductible in the settlement of the Calculation Period that is being 
settled, and another Technical Advance may be requested and charged to the next settlement. 
f) Initial Expenses Loan: if the Initial Expenses Loan is used, pursuant to the provisions of section 
3.4.3.2. of the Additional Building Block, the interest on the Initial Expenses Loan will be 
recorded in each period in accordance with the accrual criteria. 
g) Derivative Contracts: Derivative Contracts serve to cover the interest rate risk to which the 
Fund is exposed on account of the difference between the reference interest rates of its assets and 
liabilities. The proceeds of these Contracts are recorded in the income statement symmetrically to 
the proceeds of the covered elements. 
Accounting period: the accounting periods of the Fund will start on 1 January and end on 31 
December each year, except the first accounting period, which will start on the Date of 
Incorporation, and the last accounting period, which will end on the date that the Fund is 
extinguished.

4.4.3. 
Early liquidation and extinction of the Fund 
Notwithstanding the above, pursuant to the future provisions of the Articles of 
Incorporation and the provisions of this Prospectus, the Sociedad Gestora will be 
authorised to proceed to carry out the early liquidation of the Fund and hence the early 
redemption of the Bonds, when on a Payment Date (as such is defined in section 4.8.1. of 
the Securities Note) the sum of the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the Participations 
and Certificates is less than 10% of the original balance thereof, and provided that (i) the 
authorization necessary to do so has been obtained from the competent authorities; and 
(ii) the liquidation of the Participations and the Certificates pending repayment, together 
with the balance that exists at that time in the Fund Accounts (Treasury Account, 
Collection Account, Liquidity Line Sinking Account and, where applicable, in the 
Reinvestment Accounts and in the Treasury Surplus Account), permits the full repayment 
of all the outstanding obligations vis-à-vis the Security holders, in accordance with the 
provisions of this section, and respecting any prior payments that are to be given priority, 
in accordance with the Payment Priority Order. 
It is understood, in all cases, that payment obligations derived from the Securities on the 
Early Liquidation Date mean the Receivable Nominal Balance of the Securities on that 
date, plus the unpaid accrued interest to that date, amounts that to all legal effects will be 
deemed at that date past due and payable. 
The Fund will be extinguished following the liquidation of the remaining assets, in any 
event, in the following circumstances, and the CNMV and the Rating Agencies will be 
informed beforehand if any of them occur: 
(i) 
When, in the opinion of the Sociedad Gestora, exceptional circumstances occur 
which make it impossible, or extremely difficult, to maintain the financial balance of 
the Fund.  
(ii) In the event that the Sociedad Gestora is declared bankrupt and the time limit 
established by law for such purposes, or else four months, have elapsed without a 
new sociedad gestora having been designated according to the provisions of section 
3.7.2.2. of the Additional Building Block. 
 (iii) When there occurs a non-payment indicative of a serious and permanent imbalance 
in relation to the securities issued or it is foreseen that it is going to occur.  
(iv) When there is a change in the tax regulations, in accordance with the regulations 
applicable to the Fund and to the Securities that, in the opinion of the Sociedad 
Gestora, has a significant and negative effect on the financial balance of the Fund. 
(v) When thirty (30) months elapse since the date of maturity of the last Mortgage Loan 
pooled in the Fund, even if debits remain unpaid. 
The Fund will be extinguished, in any event, as a result of the following circumstances:

4.6. 
Fund tax system 
There follows a brief summary of the general tax regulations applicable to the Fund. This must be 
construed without prejudice to the particular nature of each local jurisdiction and of the regulations 
which may apply at the time the relevant income is obtained or declared. 
The tax regime applicable to Fondos de Titulización de Activos (Asset Securitization Funds) 
consists of the general provisions contained in Legislative Royal Decree 4/2004 of 5 March 
approving the consolidated text of Corporate Income Tax (Impuesto sobre Sociedades) and its 
implementing provisions, with the specific peculiarities arising from the provisions of Act 19/1992 
of 7 July regulating Sociedades y Fondos de Inversión Inmobiliaria y sobre Fondos de Titulización 
Hipotecaria (Real Estate Investment Funds and Companies and Mortgage Backed Securitization 
Funds - “Ley 19/1992”), in Act 3/1994 of 14 April, adapting Spanish legislation on credit 
institutions to the Second Directive on Banking Coordination and introducing other changes 
regarding the financial system (“Ley 3/1994”) and in Royal Decree 926/1998 which, in summary, 
define the following fundamental principles: 
1) 
Asset Securitization Funds are liable to Corporate Income Tax, subject to the general 
rules for determining the tax base, and to the general rate of 35 percent, and to the 
common rules for deductions, set-off of losses and other substantive elements of the tax. 
2) 
Investment income from Securitization Funds is subject to the general rules on 
withholdings on account of Corporate Income Tax, with the particularity that article 57-
k of the Regulations approved by Royal Decree 1777/2004, of 30 July stipulates that 
withholding does not apply to “income from mortgage participating units, mortgage 
loans and other credit rights that constitute revenue items for Securitization Funds". 
Consequently, in addition to the income from the directly securitised Participations and 
Certificates, the withholding exemption also extends, according to the expressly stated 
policy of the tax administration, to the income of the Mortgage Loans, insofar as they 
form part of the ordinary business activity of the said funds. 
3) 
Article 5.10 of Ley 19/1992 provides that the formation of mortgage securitization funds 
is exempt from classification as “corporate operations”, from Stamp Duty and from 
Real Estate Transfer Tax, thereby predetermining its submission to the same. 
The transfer to the Fund of the Participations and the Certificates stipulated in the 
Articles of Incorporation as described above is a transaction that is subject to but 
exempt from Value Added Tax (“VAT”), pursuant to the provisions of article 
20.One.18-e of the Value Added Tax Act 37/1992 of 28 December (“Ley del IVA”). 
The establishment and assignment of guarantees is subject to the general tax regime 
with no exceptions. 
4) 
In relation to Value Added Tax, the Fund will be subject to the general rules, with the 
sole particularity that the services provided for the Fund by the Sociedad Gestora will be 
exempt from Value Added Tax, and from Stamp Duty.

The Securities Issue will be exempt from VAT (article 20.One.18 of Ley del IVA) and

5. BUSINESS OVERVIEW 
5.1. 
Brief description of the issuer’s main activities 
As described throughout this Prospectus, the Fund will be set up as a vehicle intended to carry out 
a concrete transaction, pursuing the principal activities summarised below and explained in detail 
throughout this Prospectus: 
a) 
The Fund, on its Date of Incorporation, will acquire, by means of the issue by the 
Sellers of the Participations and the Certificates, a portfolio of Mortgage Loans owned 
by the Sellers, the main characteristics of which are described in the Additional 
Building Block. 
b) 
To pay the price of that acquisition, the Fund will issue, on that same date, the 
Securities, for the amounts determined in section 4.2. of the Securities Note.  
c) 
The Reserve Fund will be created on the Disbursement Date with part of the Securities 
issue price. 
d) 
In addition, on the same Date of Incorporation, it will enter into a number of contracts 
needed for the administration and management of the Fund and for the subscription and 
management of the Securities issued, which will be described throughout this 
Prospectus:  
- 
Initial Expenses Loan Contract,  
- 
Derivative Contracts,   
- 
Liquidity Line Contract,  
- 
Financial Services Contract with BANCO SANTANDER CENTRAL HISPANO, 
S.A. (“SCH” or the “Paying Agent”), for handling payment of the interest and 
principal of the Securities on the relevant dates, including the Securities 
Disbursement Date; additionally, SCH will be the depository of the Multiple 
Certificates and the Fund Accounts, except, where applicable, the Reinvestment 
Accounts, which will be held by the appropriately Rated Sellers and the Treasury 
Surplus Account, which will be opened in another appropriately rated entity; and 
- 
Placement Subscription and Underwriting Contract with BSIL, EBN BANCO and 
SOCIÉTÉ GÉNÉRALE, for underwriting the Bonds and placing them with qualified 
investors.

6. ADMINISTRATION, MANAGEMENT AND SUPERVISORY BODIES 
6.1. 
Management, administration and representation of the Issuer 
As provided by Royal Decree 926/1998, the Fund will be legally represented and managed by its 
Sociedad Gestora, TITULIZACIÓN DE ACTIVOS, S.G.F.T., S.A.  
The registered name of the Sociedad Gestora is Titulización de Activos, Sociedad Gestora de 
Fondos de Titulización, S.A., with Tax Identification Number (C.I.F.) A-80352750. 
The Sociedad Gestora is a Spanish public limited company (sociedad anónima), incorporated on 
12 May 1992, with registered office at C/Orense, 69 Madrid (Spain), (Tel: +34 91 702 08 08), and 
registered in the Mercantile Registry of Madrid, Volume 4280, book 0, folio 183, Section 8, sheet 
M-71066, entry nº 5, on 4 June, 1993, and also registered under number 3 in the Registro Especial 
de Sociedades Gestoras de Fondos de Titulización Hipotecaria (Special Register of Mortgage 
Securitization Fund Management Companies) kept by the CNMV.  
The Sociedad Gestora has been incorporated for an indefinite period of time, unless any of the 
grounds stipulated by law for its winding-up occurs.

6.2. 
Audit of the financial statements of the Sociedad Gestora 
The Sociedad Gestora has accounts for 2002, 2003 and 2004 audited by Ernst & Young, which 
have been filed at the CNMV and at the Mercantile Registry. The audit reports on the annual 
financial statements for 2002, 2003 and 2004 contained no qualifications. The financial statements 
of the Sociedad Gestora are audited by Ernst & Young, S.L., whose details are given in section 
5.2. of the Registration Document.  
6.3. 
Principal activities 
The sole purpose of the Sociedad Gestora is the incorporation, management and legal 
representation of Fondos de Titulización de Activos and Fondos de Titulización Hipotecaria, in 
accordance with the provisions of Royal Decree 926/1998. 
TITULIZACIÓN DE ACTIVOS, SGFT, S.A. will be responsible for the administration and legal 
representation of the Fund, in accordance with the provisions of Royal Decree 926/1998 and Ley 
19/1992 vis-à-vis any aspects not covered by Royal Decree 926/1998, when applicable, and the 
rest of the applicable legal regulations, as well as the provisions of the Articles of Incorporation. 
The Sociedad Gestora will perform for the Fund those duties attributed to it in Royal Decree 
926/1998. As the manager of third party funds, the Sociedad Gestora is also responsible for 
representing and safeguarding the interests of holders of Bonds issued by the Fund and its other 
ordinary creditors. Consequently, the Sociedad Gestora must subordinate its actions to 
safeguarding the interests of such persons, abiding by the applicable provisions in this regard 
prevailing from time to time. The Security holders and remaining creditors of the Fund will have 
no recourse against the Sociedad Gestora, other than from non-performance of its duties or non-
compliance with the provisions of the Articles of Incorporation and this Prospectus.   
On the date of registration of this Prospectus, the Sociedad Gestora, has a total of 58 securitization 
funds under management, the details of which are given in section 6.8. of this Registration 
Document. 
6.4. 
Existence or non-existence of holdings in other companies 
The Sociedad Gestora does not hold equity interests in any company. 
6.5. 
Entities from which the Sociedad Gestora has borrowed more than 10% 
The Sociedad Gestora has not been granted any financing by third parties. 
6.6. 
Litigation of the Sociedad Gestora 
At the date of registration of this Prospectus, there are no disputes, litigation or bankruptcy-related 
situation liable to have a material effect on the economic and financial situation of the Sociedad 
Gestora or on its future capacity to perform the Fund management and administration duties 
stipulated in this Prospectus. 
6.7. 
Administration, management and supervisory bodies 
Pursuant to the provisions of the articles of association of the Sociedad Gestora, and at the date of 
registration of this Prospectus, the Sociedad Gestora has no governing bodies other than the 
Shareholders' Meeting and the Board of Directors.

4. INFORMATION CONCERNING THE SECURITIES TO BE OFFERED 
AND ADMITTED TO TRADING 
4.1. 
Total amount of the securities 
The total face value of the mortgage-backed bonds issue (the “Bonds”) will be FOUR HUNDRED 
AND EIGHTY-FIVE MILLION (485,000,000) euros), formed by four thousand eight hundred 
and fifty (4,850) Bonds, each with a unit face value of one hundred thousand (100,000) euros.  
4.2. 
Description of the type and class of the securities 
4.2.1. 
Type and class of securities 
This Securities Note is issued for the purposes of the issue of the Fund Securities. 
The Securities represent a debt for the Fund, accrue interest and are redeemable through 
early redemption or at final maturity. The Bonds and the NAS-IO Securities legally 
qualify as marketable fixed interest securities with an explicit yield and are subject to the 
provisions of the Ley del Mercado de Valores and the regulations in development thereof.  
The total amount of the Bond Issue is grouped in four (4) Series as follows: 
a)  Class A: the Class A Bonds will be issued in two (2) Series, for a total nominal 
amount of FOUR HUNDRED AND FIFTY-EIGHT MILLION FOUR 
HUNDRED THOUSAND (458,400,000) euros, formed by FOUR THOUSAND 
FIVE HUNDRED AND EIGHTY-FOUR (4,584) Bonds, each with a unit face 
value of one hundred thousand (100,000) euros, represented by book entries 
(referred to either as the “Series A” or the “Series A Bonds”), formed by: 
- 
Series A1 Bonds, for a total nominal amount of THREE HUNDRED 
AND SIXTY-ONE MILLION FOUR HUNDRED THOUSAND 
(361,400,000) euros, formed by THREE THOUSAND SIX HUNDRED 
AND FOURTEEN (3,614) Bonds, each with a face value of one hundred 
thousand (100,000) euros, represented by book entries (referred to either 
as the “Series A1” or the “Series A1 Bonds”); and 
- 
Series A2 Bonds, for a total nominal amount of NINETY SEVEN 
MILLION (97,000,000) euros, formed by ONE THOUSAND (1,000) 
Bonds, each with a unit face value of one hundred thousand (100,000) 
euros, represented by book entries (referred to either as the “Series A2” 
or the “Series A2 Bonds”). These Bonds will be issued for between 
104.1% and (106%) of their face value, that is to say, for an amount 
between ONE HUNDRED MILLION NINE HUNDRED AND 
SEVENTY SEVEN THOUSAND (100,977,000) euros and ONE 
HUNDRED AND TWO MILLION EIGHT HUNDRED AND TWENTY 
THOUSAND (102,820,000) euros. 
The issue price of the A2 Bonds will be determined by the Lead 
Managers, at the latest, before 13:00 hours (CET time) on the second 
(2nd) Business Day before the Disbursement Date (that is to say, 29

Informativo" drafted in the Spanish language is the only official document, and no document other than the "Folleto Informativo"shall have 
any legal effect or be relied upon with regard to the Note Issue.

November 2005) and will be reported by fax to the Sociedad Gestora

In the absence of such notification, the Sociedad Gestora will set the issue 
price of the A2 Bonds as 104.1% of their face value, that is to say, an 
amount equal to ONE HUNDRED MILLION NINE HUNDRED AND 
NINETY SEVEN THOUSAND (100,977,000) euros. At the same time 
the Sociedad Gestora will also notify the CNMV of this additional 
information to the Prospectus. The final spread applicable will be 
registered in the disbursement certificate. 
 
b) Class B: the Class B Bonds will be issued in Series B, for a total nominal amount 
of THIRTEEN MILLION FIVE HUNDRED THOUSAND (13,500,000) euros, 
formed by ONE HUNDRED AND THIRTY-FIVE (135) Bonds, each with a unit 
face value of one hundred thousand (100,000) euros, represented by book entries 
(referred to either as the “Series B” or the “Series Bonds”). 
c) Class C: the Class C Bonds will be issued in Series C, for a total nominal amount 
of EIGHT MILLION ONE HUNDRED THOUSAND (8,100,000) euros, formed 
by EIGHTY ONE (81) Bonds, each with a unit face value of one hundred 
thousand (100,000) euros, represented by book entries (referred to either as the 
“Series C” or the “Series C Bonds”). 
d) Class D: the Class D Bonds will be issued in Series D, for a total nominal 
amount of FIVE MILLION (5,000,000) euros, formed by FIFTY (50) Bonds, 
each with a unit face value of one hundred thousand (100,000) euros, represented 
by book entries (referred to either as the “Series D” or the “Series D Bonds”). 
The Series of A1, B, C and D Bonds are issued at par with their face value.. 
Additionally, on the Date of Incorporation, part of the interest of the Series A2 Bonds will 
be segregated, as is described in section 4.8. of the Securities Note, into Non-
Amortization Senior Interest-Only Securities (the “NAS-IO Securities”) that will consist 
on the Date of Incorporation of NINE HUNDRED SEVENTY (970) securities, each with 
a notional amount equal to the face value of each of the Series A2 Bonds, that is to say, 
one hundred thousand (100,000) euros. During the Subscription Period, each of the Series 
A2 Bonds will be subscribed and will involve the payment on the Disbursement Date of 
(i) one hundred thousand (100,000) euros, by the subscribers of the Series A2 Bonds; and 
(ii) an amount that will be between four thousand and one hundred euros (4,100 euros) 
and six thousand euros (6,000 euros), for each NAS-IO Security subscribed. On each 
Payment Date, the notional amount of the NAS-IO securities will equal the Outstanding 
Nominal Balance of the Series A2 Bonds. 
The price of each NAS-IO Security will be determined by the Lead Managers, at the 
latest, before 13:00 hours (CET time) on the second (2nd) Business Day before the 
Disbursement Date and before the start of the Subscription Period (that is to say, 29 
November 2005) and will be reported by fax to the Sociedad Gestora before 13:00 hours 
(CET time) on 29 November 2005 by the Lead Managers.  
If such notice is not given, the Sociedad Gestora will establish the price of each NAS-IO 
Security as FOUR THOUSAND AND ONE HUNDRED EUROS (4,100 euros). At the 
same time the Sociedad Gestora will also notify the CNMV of this additional information

price, but only the right to collect, until it matures, the NAS-IO Payment, always subject 
to the Payment Priority Order. 
Subscribing or holding Securities of one series does not imply subscribing or holding 
Securities of the other Series. This mention also applies to the NAS-IO Securities with 
regard to other Series of Bonds.

The Underwriting and Placement Agents will assume the obligations contained in the 
Placement Subscription and Underwriting Contract, namely the following:  
1) 
procuring the third-party placing and subscription of the Securities;  
2) 
commitment to subscribe for their own account the Securities that have not 
been subscribed by third parties during the Subscription Period, up to the 
total amounts of their respective pooled underwriting commitments;  
3) 
payment by the Underwriting and Placement Agents to the Paying Agent on 
the Disbursement Date, before 11:00 hours (CET) and for value that same 
day, the nominal value of the Securities placed by each of them and, as 
applicable, subscribed by them for their own account up to their respective 
underwriting commitments, whereupon the Paying Agent will pay to the 
Fund, before 12:00 hours (CET), for value that same day, the amount paid 
thereto by the Underwriting and Placement Agents; 
4) 
commitment to pay the default interest agreed in the contract in the event of 
delay in the payment of the amounts owed;  
5) 
delivery to the subscribers of a document evidencing the subscription;  
6) 
delivery to the Paying Agent of the information about the control of the 
dissemination achieved in placing the Bonds; and 
7) 
other matters regulating the underwriting and placement 
The placement of the Securities will take place during the Subscription Period, which will 
run from the previous Business Day to the Disbursement Date at 10:00 a.m. (CET time) 
to the Disbursement Date (1 December 2005) at 10:00 a.m. (CET time). Such placement 
and allocation will be performed at BSIL’s free discretion, taking into account the 
instructions received from the other Underwriting and Placement Agents. Such entity may 
place the underwritten Securities at its discretion, taking into account the instructions 
received from the other Underwriting and Placement Agents, according to the nature of 
the issuance and the common practice in these markets, and ensuring that there is no 
discrimination between requests of similar characteristics. Notwithstanding the foregoing, 
BSIL may give priority to any of its clients’ requests that it deems necessary, albeit 
always taking into consideration the instructions received from the other Underwriting 
and Placement Agents. The obligation acquired by the Underwriting and Placement 
Agents is pooled and irrevocable, such that each one of them is liable solely for the 
amount it has respectively underwritten. 
Without prejudice to the provisions of the previous paragraph, the non-confirmation 
before the start of the Subscription Period of the provisional ratings assigned to the 
Securities by the Rating Agencies as well as the occurrence, before the start of the said 
Subscription Period, of an event that could not be foreseen or that, despite being 
foreseeable, could not be avoided and makes it impossible to perform the Fund's 
Contracts pursuant to the provisions of section 1,105 of the Civil Code, will both be 
construed as grounds for termination of the incorporation of the Fund, the issue of the

The Fund has been incorporated and the Securities are being issued in accordance with the Spanish 
law applicable to the Fund or to the Securities. In particular, they are being issued in accordance 
with the provisions of (i) the Ley del Mercado de Valores 24/1988, (Securities Market Act) of 28 
July, (ii) Royal Decree 926/1998 and its implementing provisions and Ley 19/1992 as to matters 
not provided for in Royal Decree 926/1998 and insofar as applicable, (iii) Royal Decree 
1310/2005, of 4 November, partially implementing the Ley del Mercado de Valores, with regard to 
the admission of Securities to trading on official secondary markets, initial and secondary public 
offerings and the prospectus that must be issued for these purposes and (iv) other statutory 
provisions and regulatory in force and that apply from time to time.

The Securities will only be represented by book entries, pursuant to the provisions of article 11 of

in IBERCLEAR. In this respect, it is hereby stated that the Articles of Incorporation will produce 
the effect set forth in article 6 of the Ley del Mercado de Valores. 
IBERCLEAR will be appointed as the entity in charge of the Security bookkeeping in the Articles 
of Incorporation, such that the Securities are cleared and settled in accordance with the rules of 
procedure established or that may be approved in the future by IBERCLEAR or AIAF relating to 
securities admitted to trading in AIAF and represented by book entries. 
The Security holders will be identified in accordance with the book entries made by the entities 
that participate in IBERCLEAR.

and CLEARSTREAM, although the Sociedad Gestora may also apply for their registration by 
other European Stock markets, as it deems appropriate.

Currency of the issue 
The Securities will be denominated in euros. 
4.6. 
Ranking of the securities according to the subordination rules 
4.6.1. 
Simple mention of the ranking of the Security interest payments in the Fund order 
of payments 
The payment of interest of the Class A Bonds and the NAS-IO payment will rank sixth 
(6th) in the Payment Priority Order established in section 3.4.6. of the Additional Building 
Block. 
The payment of the interest accrued by the Series B Bonds ranks seventh (7th) in the 
Payment Priority Order established in section 3.4.6. of the Additional Building Block, 
unless the circumstances stipulated in the same section for its deferral occur, in which 
case it will rank eleventh (11th). 
The payment of the interest accrued by the Series C Bonds ranks eighth (8th) in the 
Payment Priority Order established in section 3.4.6. of the Additional Building Block, 
unless the circumstances stipulated in the same section for its deferral occur, in which 
case it will rank eleventh (12th). 
The payment of the interest accrued by the Series D Bonds ranks eighth (9th) in the 
Payment Priority Order established in section 3.4.6. of the Additional Building Block, 
unless the circumstances stipulated in the same section for its deferral occur, in which 
case it will rank twelfth (13th).

4.7. 
Description of the rights attached to the securities 
Pursuant to current legislation, the Securities detailed in the present Securities Note will offer no 
future or present voting right to the investor over the Fund or its Sociedad Gestora. 
The Investor's economic and financial rights associated with the acquisition and ownership of the 
Securities will be those derived from the interest rates, yields and redemption prices with which 
the Securities are issued and which are detailed in sections 4.8. and 4.9. infra in this Securities 
Note. 
The Security holders are subject, with respect to the payment of interest and repayment of the 
principal and to the NAS-IO Payments, to the Payment Priority Order. 
The Security holders will have no recourse against the Sociedad Gestora, other than from non-
performance of its duties or non-compliance with the provisions of this Prospectus, of the Articles 
of Incorporation and the applicable laws and regulations. 
Any dispute regarding the Fund that may arise during its operations or liquidation, be it amongst 
the Security holders or between the latter and the Sociedad Gestora, will be submitted to the courts 
and tribunals of Spain, with waiver of any other jurisdiction to which the parties may be entitled. 
4.8. 
The nominal interest rate and provisions relating to interest payable 
Interest on the Securities 
All the Bonds issued will accrue a nominal, annual and quarterly-variable interest on the 
Outstanding Nominal Balance of the Bonds on each Payment Date, and payable each quarter 
(“Nominal Interest Rate”), from the Disbursement Date and until they are fully redeemed, while 
the NAS-IO Securities will accrue a fixed interest calculated on their notional amount, as 
explained below. The interest of the Bonds, whatever their Class and Series, and the NAS-IO 
Payments will be payable at the end of each quarter on each Payment Date.  
The interest of the Securities will be paid, in relation to the other Fund payments, in the Payment 
Priority Order set forth in section 3.4.6. of the Additional Building Block.  
For interest accrual purposes, the Securities issue will be divided into successive interest accrual 
periods (hereinafter, “Interest Accrual Periods”) which will include the days elapsed between 
each Payment Date (including the initial Payment Date and excluding the final Payment Date). 
The first Interest Accrual Period will start on (and include) the Disbursement Date and will end on 
(and exclude) the first Payment Date, 22 March 2006. 
The Nominal Rate of Interest accrued by each Series of A1, B, C and D Bonds during each Interest 
Accrual Period will be the result of adding (i) the Reference Interest Rate, calculated as stipulated 
below, and common to all Bond Series, and rounded to the nearest thousandth, taking into account 
that, in the event of equal conditions for rounding up or down, the amount will always be rounded 
up, plus (ii) the spread applicable to each Series of A1, B, C and D Bonds, as indicated below. 
Part of the interest of Series A2 Bonds will be segregated on the Date of Incorporation in NAS-IO 
Securities, as described in this section.

Reference Rate of interest 
The Reference Interest Rate for setting the interest rate applicable to the Bonds of all Series will be 
the three (3) month EURIBOR interest rate or, if necessary, its substitute (the “Reference Interest 
Rate”), determined as stated below.  
Fixing of the Bond Reference Interest Rate 
The EURIBOR will be fixed according to the rules established in this section. 
On each Fixing Date, the Sociedad Gestora will fix the Reference Interest Rate, which will be 
equal to the EURIBOR, as follows:  
(i) 
The 3-month EURIBOR interest rate on the page EURIBOR= of the REUTERS screen, 
on the Fixing Date at 11:00 a.m. (CET time). “REUTERS screen, "EURIBOR page" is 
the one that displays the contents of the "EURIBOR page" on the REUTERS MONITOR 
MONEY RATES SERVICE (or any other page that may replace it in this service). 
(ii) In the absence of rates as indicated in section (i) supra, the three (3) month EURIBOR on 
the “TELERATE” screen (TELERATE SPAIN, S.A.), on page 248, or any other page 
that may be used instead on the Fixing Date at 11:00 a.m. (CET time) will prevail. 
(iii) In the absence of rates as indicated in sections (i) and (ii) supra, the simple arithmetic 
mean of London interbank rates for non transferable deposits in euros, with three (3) 
month maturity, for an amount equivalent to the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the 
Bonds offered on the Fixing Date by the entities mentioned below, after and at about 
11:00 a.m. (CET time) will prevail. This interest rate will be requested simultaneously 
from the following entities: 
- 
Banco Santander Central Hispano (London) 
- 
JP Morgan Chase & Co. (London) 
- 
Barclays Bank (London) 
- 
Confederación Española de Cajas de Ahorros (London Branch) 
In the event that one or several of the aforementioned institutions do not furnish a list of 
quoted rates, the rate applied will be the rate that results from applying the simple 
arithmetic mean of the rates declared by at least two of the remaining institutions.  
(iv) In the absence of rates as indicated in sections (i), (ii), and (iii), the rate applied will be 
the Reference Interest Rate of the immediately previous Interest Accrual Period, and so 
on for the following Interest Accrual Periods insofar as the situation remains unchanged. 
If the Reference Interest Rate is not published as specified in sections (i), (ii) and (iii) 
supra on the first Fixing Date, the rate applied will be the rate published, in accordance 
with the provisions of section (i), on the last Business Day on which such Reference 
Interest Rate has been published. 
The Sociedad Gestora will keep the listings of the contents of the REUTERS or TELERATE 
screens or, where applicable, the rates quoted by the institutions mentioned in section (iii) supra, 
as evidence of the EURIBOR rate applied.

Notwithstanding the above, the Reference Rate of Interest for the first Interest Accrual Period, in 
other words, the period between the Disbursement Date and the first Payment Date, will be the 
result of the linear interpolation between the three (3) month EURIBOR rate and the four (4) 
month EURIBOR rate, taking into account the number of days of the first Interest Accrual Period. 
The Interest Rate for the first Interest Accrual Period will be calculated with the following 
formula: 
R= E3 + (21/31) * (E4-E3) 
Where: 
R= Reference Interest Rate for the first Interest Accrual Period. 
E3= three (3) month EURIBOR rate. 
E4= four (4) month EURIBOR rate. 
The three (3) month EURIBOR rate for the first Accrual Period will be determined in accordance 
with the rules established in the previous paragraphs of this section and the four (4) month 
EURIBOR rate will be determined in accordance with the same rules, although the time references 
made beforehand will change, accordingly, from three (3) to four (4) months, with the exception of 
the rule stipulated in section (iv) supra, which will not apply. 
Reference Interest Rate Fixing Date  
The Reference Interest Rate Fixing Date for each Interest Accrual Period will be the second (2nd) 
Business Day prior to the Payment Date in question ("Fixing Date") and will apply for the next 
Interest Accrual Period. For the first Interest Accrual Period, the Reference Interest Rate will be 
determined on 29 November 2005, before the start of the Subscription Period. 
Once the Reference Interest Rate has been fixed, and on the same Fixing Date, the Sociedad 
Gestora will calculate and fix, for each of the Series of Bonds, the Nominal Interest Rate 
applicable to the next Interest Accrual Period. 
Spread applicable to the Reference Interest Rate for each Series of Bonds 
The spread applicable to the Series A1, A2, B, C and D Bonds, expressed as a percentage, will be 
determined by common consent by the Lead Managers, at the latest, before 13:00 hours (CET 
time) on the second (2nd) Business Day before the Disbursement Date (that is to say, 29 November 
2005). The definitive spread applicable to the Bonds will be reported by fax to the Sociedad 
Gestora before 13:00 hours (CET time) on 29 November 2005 by the Lead Managers. The spreads 
that will be applied to each of the Series A1, A2, B, C and D to calculate the rate of interest that 
will accrue in each Interest Accrual Period will range as follows:

4.8.1. 
Time limit on the validity of claims to interest and repayment of principal 
The interest of the Bonds, whatever their Class and Series, and the NAS-IO Payments 
will be payable at the end of each quarter, on 22 March, 22 June, 22 September and 22 
December of each year until the full maturity of the Securities. If any of these days is not 
a Business Day, the interest and principal for that quarter (except for the first Payment 
Date, which will be the interest and principal for the time elapsed between the 
Disbursement Date and the first Payment Date) will be paid the next Business Day (each 
of these dates, a “Payment Date”). The first Payment Date will be 22 March 2006. 
For the purposes of this Securities Issue, business days (“Business Days”) are all those 
days that are not non-business days on the TARGET (Trans European Automated Real-
Time Gross Settlement Express Transfer System) calendar. 
In the event that on a Payment Date, and despite the mechanisms established for the 
protection of the rights of the Security holders, the Available Funds were insufficient to 
satisfy the Fund interest payment obligations as specified in section 3.4.6. of the 
Additional Building Block, the amount available for the interest payment will be 
distributed in accordance with the Payment Priority Order stipulated in the 
aforementioned section and in the event that the Available Funds are only enough to 
partially pay obligations that rank in the same priority order, the amount available will be 
distributed among the Securities involved in proportion to their Outstanding Nominal 
Balance, and any amounts that the Security holders have not received will be paid on the 
next Payment Date when it is possible, without accruing additional interest. In this 
respect, the NAS-IO payment will be construed as Series A2 Bond interest and the 
amount that is allocated will be distributed between the Series A2 Bonds and the NAS-IO 
Securities (in the case of the NAS-IO Payment) in proportion to the amounts owed on 
such grounds. The payments outstanding to the Security holders will be made on the next

Description of the underlying security on which the interest rate and historic

The Reference Rate of Interest for determining the Nominal Interest Rate applicable to 
each of the Series of Bonds is as described in section 4.8. of this Securities Note. 
At present, the Euribor rate is the Euro interbank offered rate calculated as the daily 
average of the rates provided for fifteen maturity terms by a panel of 57 of the most active 
Euro zone banks. The rate is quoted on the basis of true days to maturity and 360 day-
years, and is fixed at 11:00 hours (CET) expressed with three (3) decimal points. 
Any Euribor-related definitions that might be approved by the Fédération Bancaire de 
l’Union Européenne (FBE) and by the Association Cambiste Internationale (ACI - 
Financial Markets Association) and that complement the existing definition of the 
Euribor, will be deemed to be included in the effects of the Reference Interest Rate 
relating to the Euribor without any need for these terms of the Reference Interest Rate to 
be modified or for the Security holders to be notified by the Sociedad Gestora. 
Solely for information purposes, there follow the data of the three (3) month Euribor rates 
published on the dates indicated, on the Reuters screen "EURIBOR=" page, as well as the

and of 1.75% for the Series D Bonds):

4.8.3. 
Calculation Agent 
The Sociedad Gestora will be the agent responsible for calculating the interest on the 
Securities. 
4.9. 
Maturity date and redemption of the securities 
4.9.1. 
Redemption price 
The Bonds will be redeemed at 100% of their face value, that is to say, 100,000 euros per 
Bond, free of costs and taxes for the Bondholder, payable progressively on each principal 
Payment Date, as set forth in section 4.9.2. infra of this Securities Note. The holders of 
the NAS-IO Securities are not entitled to reimbursement of the subscription price, as is 
indicated in section 4.8. of this Securities Note. 
4.9.2. 
Date and types of redemption 
4.9.2.1 
Redemption of the Bonds  
Amount to be Redeemed  
The redemption of the Bonds will be conducted on a pro rata basis among the Bonds of 
the same Series that are scheduled for redemption on each Payment Date (as provided for 
below), by reducing the nominal amount, until it has been completed, by an amount equal 
to the smaller of the following amounts:  
(a) The positive difference on that Payment Date between the Outstanding Nominal 
Balance of the Bonds (before the amount redeemed on that Payment Date) and 
the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the non-defaulted Participations and the 
Certificates for the last day of the month prior to the month of the Payment Date, 
and 
(b)  the Available Funds on that Payment Date, after deducting the amounts of the 
preceding items in the Payment Priority Order. 
Consequently, in the event of defaulted Participations and Certificates (those whose 
Mortgage Loans are 12 months or more in arrears), the Bonds will be redeemed by an 
amount equal to their Nominal Balance Outstanding on the last day of the calendar month 
prior to the current Payment Date, plus the amounts due and uncollected from the 
aforementioned Payment Date until the last day of the calendar month prior to the current 
Payment Date. The Bonds will be redeemed using the Available Funds, always after 
paying any obligations that rank before the redemption in the Payment Priority Order. 
Should there not be any Available Funds for making these payments, the corresponding 
amounts will remain pending redemption until the immediately next Payment Date. 
Should it not be possible to substitute the Participations and Certificates, as stipulated in 
section 2.2.9. of the Additional Building Block, the proceeds of the early redemption, by 
the Sellers, of the Participations and/or Certificates in question, will form part of the 
Available Funds that will be applied on the next Payment Date. 
Sequential redemption 
The Bonds will be redeemed sequentially, such that the redemption of the Series A1 
Bonds will commence on the first Payment Date (22 March 2006) and the redemption of

the Series A2 Bonds will only commence when the Series A1 Bonds have been redeemed 
in full. 
The redemption of the Series B Bonds will only commence when the Class A Bonds have 
been redeemed in full.  
The redemption of the Series C Bonds will only commence when the Class B Bonds have 
been redeemed in full. 
And the redemption of the Series D Bonds will only commence when the Class C Bonds 
have been redeemed in full. 
Pro rata redemption requirements 
Notwithstanding the above, the amount to be redeemed will be distributed pro rata among 
the Class A, B, C and D Bonds in proportion to the Outstanding Nominal Balance of each 
of the Bonds, when the following circumstances occur simultaneously on a Payment 
Date: 
(1) that the ratio between the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the Series B, C and 
D Bonds, together, and the Outstanding Nominal Balance of all the Bonds, is 
twice the ratio between the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the Series B, C 
and D Bonds, together, and the Outstanding Nominal Balance of all the Bonds 
on the Date of Incorporation, 
(2) that the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the Non-Defaulted Participations and 
Certificates more than 90 days in arrears represents less than 1.5% of the 
Outstanding Nominal Balance of the total of the Non-Defaulted Participations 
and Certificates pooled in the Fund at that time, 
(3) that the Reserve Fund meets the required level , and 
(4) that, in the event that the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the Participations 
and the Certificates represents less than 10% of their Outstanding Nominal 
Balance on the Incorporation Date, the Sociedad Gestora does not decide to 
proceed with the early liquidation of the Fund. 
Payment of the Class A Bonds with allocation on a pro rata basis 
In this event, following the pro rata allocation among all the Bonds, the amount 
applicable, on that Payment Date, to the redemption of the Series A1 and A2 Bonds, will 
only be used to redeem the Series A1 Bonds, until they are fully redeemed. When the 
Series A1 Bonds have been redeemed, the amount applicable will be used to redeem the 
Series A2 Bonds, until they are fully redeemed.  
Exceptional rules regarding redemption of the Class A Bonds 
Exceptionally, if on a Payment Date, the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the Non-
Defaulted Participations and Certificates more than 90 days in arrears represents 3% or 
more of the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the total of the Non-Defaulted Participations 
and Certificates pooled in the Fund, the amount to be allocated to redemption of the Class 
A Bonds will be allocated on a pro rata basis to the Series A1 and A2 Bonds.  
The pro rata redemption of the Series A1 and A2 Bonds will continue provided that, on 
each Payment Date, the aforementioned arrears percentage remains at or exceeds 3%, 
otherwise the Series A1 and A2 Bonds will be redeemed sequentially again, as described 
above.

4.9.2.2 
Collection Dates, Calculation Dates, Calculation Periods and Notification 
Dates 
“Collection Date”, will be each of the dates on which the Sellers, as servicers of their 
respective mortgage loans, will pay the amounts received from such Mortgage Loans into 
the Collection Account. CAJA CASTILLA LA MANCHA and CREDIFIMO will make 
their payments on a weekly basis, each Tuesday or, if is not a Business Day, on the 
immediately next Business Day. BANKPIME will make its payments on the 4th and 19th 
of each month or, if either of these is not a Business Day, the immediately next Business 
Day. 
The deposits in the Collection Account may be made at different intervals, pursuant to the 
provisions of section 3.4.4.1. of the Additional Building Block. 
“Calculation Date” will mean the date on which the Sociedad Gestora will calculate the 
amount that each Seller should have delivered to it during the previous Calculation Period 
and the Technical Advance, as well as the date on which it will transfer the Collected 
Amount from the Collection Account to the Treasury Account, that is to say, the 20th of 
each month or, if it is not a Business Day, the immediately previous Business Day. The 
first Calculation Date will be 20 December 2005. 
“Calculation Period”, will mean a period that coincides with a calendar month. 
Exceptionally, the first Calculation Period will commence on the Date of Incorporation of 
the Fund and will end on the last day of the month of November 2005 (both inclusive). 
“Notification Dates”, will mean the second Business Day before each Payment Date 
throughout the life of the Fund. On these dates, the Sociedad Gestora will notify the 
amounts of principal and interest payable to the Bondholders, in the manner described in 
section 4.1.3.1. of the Additional Building Block. 
4.9.3. 
Early Redemption of the Bond Issue 
Notwithstanding the obligation of the Fund, through its Sociedad Gestora, to redeem the 
Bonds of each Series on the Legal Maturity Date (22 June 2040 or, if this is not a 
Business Day, the next Business Day) or the partial redemptions on each Payment Date, 
as established in the previous sections, the Sociedad Gestora will be authorised to proceed 
to carry out the Early Liquidation of the Fund and hence the early redemption (“Early 
Redemption”), on a Payment Date, of the entire Bond Issue, in accordance with the 
events of early liquidation and the requirements set forth in section 4.4. of the 
Registration Document and subject to the Payment Priority Order set forth in section 
3.4.6. of the Additional Building Block. 
4.10. Indication of the yield 
The main characteristic of the Bonds of this Issue is that their periodic redemption depends on the 
aggregate behaviour of the Mortgage Loans.  
The average life, yield, duration and final maturity of the Bonds of each Series and, where 
applicable, the NAS-IO Securities, depend on diverse factors, the most significant of which are as 
follows:  
a) 
 The repayment system and calendar for each of the Mortgage Loans stipulated in the 
related contracts. 


This prospectus is a translation into English of the original "Folleto Informativo" drafted in Spanish language and registered with the 
"Comisión Nacional del Mercado de Valores" (the Spanish Securities Market Commission, "CNMV") on November 25h, 2005. The "Folleto 
Informativo" drafted in the Spanish language is the only official document, and no document other than the "Folleto Informativo"shall have 
any legal effect or be relied upon with regard to the Note Issue. 
 
50 
b) 
The capacity of the Mortgagors to prepay, in full or in part, the Mortgage Loans and the 
pace at which such early redemption takes place in aggregate over the life of the Fund. 
c) 
The floating interest rates that will apply to each of the Mortgage Loans, which will cause 
the amount of each repayment instalment to vary. 
d) 
Arrears of the Mortgagors in making the Mortgage Loan repayments. 
In this regard, early redemptions by the Debtors of the Mortgage Loans are very significant. The 
early redemptions are subject to continuous change and in this Prospectus are estimated using 
several assumptions for the future behaviour of the constant annual early redemption rate 
(“ERR”). This will have a direct bearing on the pace at which the Bonds are redeemed and hence 
on their average life and duration.

been made regarding the aforesaid factors:

quarterly, taking into account the Euribor 3 months of 17 November 2005, that is to say, 
2.350%, will be maintained constant throughout the term of the loans at the following 
rates:

Note, and since the four (4) month EURIBOR rate on 17 November 2005 is 2.395% and, 
therefore the interpolated Euribor is 2.380%, the Nominal Rate of Interest applicable to the

This prospectus is a translation into English of the original "Folleto Informativo" drafted in Spanish language and registered with the 
"Comisión Nacional del Mercado de Valores" (the Spanish Securities Market Commission, "CNMV") on November 25h, 2005. The "Folleto

any legal effect or be relied upon with regard to the Note Issue.

4.11. Representation of the security holders 
No Security Holder Syndicate will be set up for the securities included in this Issue. The Security 
holders will be represented by the Sociedad Gestora in accordance with the provisions of article 12 
of Royal Decree 926/1998. Consequently, the Sociedad Gestora must subordinate its actions to 
safeguarding the interests of the holders of the Securities issued against the Fund. 
4.12. Resolutions, authorisations, and approvals for the Securities issue 
The resolutions and agreements under which these Bonds are issued, the validity whereof is 
material through the certifications sent to the CNMV, are as detailed below: 
4.12.1. Corporate resolutions 
4.12.1.1 Resolutions to transfer mortgages loans by the issue of mortgage 
participations and mortgage transfer certificates 
On 30 September 2005, the Board of Directors of CAJA CASTILLA LA MANCHA 
resolved to authorise the transfer of mortgage guarantee loans owned by the latter entity 
through the issue of mortgage participations and mortgage transfer certificates for their 
pooling or subscription by the Fund. 
On 27 October 2005, the Board of Directors of CREDIFIMO resolved to authorise the 
transfer of mortgage guarantee loans owned by the latter entity through the issue of 
mortgage participations and mortgage transfer certificates for their pooling or 
subscription by the Fund. 
On 25 October 2005, the Board of Directors of ENTITYPIME resolved to authorise the 
transfer of mortgage guarantee loans owned by the latter entity through the issue of 
mortgage participations and mortgage transfer certificates for their pooling or 
subscription by the Fund. 
4.12.1.2 Resolution to set up the Fund and issue the Bonds 
On 20 September 2005, the Board of Directors of TITULIZACIÓN DE ACTIVOS, 
S.G.F.T., S.A. resolved to incorporate the Fund in accordance with the provisions set 
forth in Royal Decree 926/1998 and in Ley 19/1992, to pool the Participations and 
Certificates issued by the Sellers over the Mortgage Loans and to issue the Securities 
against the Fund.  
4.12.2. Registration by the CNMV 
The incorporation of the Fund and the issue of the Bonds are subject to the prerequisite of 
this Prospectus and other statutory documents being filed at the Official Register of the 
CNMV, pursuant to the provisions of article 5.1.e) of Royal Decree 926/1998. 
This Prospectus was registered by the CNMV in its Official Register on 24 November 
2005.  
4.12.3. Granting of the Public Articles of Incorporation for the Fund 


This prospectus is a translation into English of the original "Folleto Informativo" drafted in Spanish language and registered with the 
"Comisión Nacional del Mercado de Valores" (the Spanish Securities Market Commission, "CNMV") on November 25h, 2005. The "Folleto 
Informativo" drafted in the Spanish language is the only official document, and no document other than the "Folleto Informativo"shall have 
any legal effect or be relied upon with regard to the Note Issue.

Once the CNMV has registered the Prospectus and before the start of the Subscription Period, the 
Sociedad Gestora, CAJA CASTILLA LA MANCHA, CREDIFIMO and BANKPIME, as sellers 
of the Participations and the Certificates to be subscribed by the Fund, will proceed to grant the 
Articles of Incorporation on the first Business Day following the date of registration of this 
Prospectus. A copy of the Articles of Incorporation will be sent to the CNMV for its registration in 
the public register, and its contents will match the contents of this Prospectus and of the draft 
Articles of Incorporation filed with the CNMV. Under no circumstances will the terms of the 
Articles of Incorporation contradict, modify, alter or render null and void the contents of such 
copy. 
4.13. Issue date of the securities  
The Securities issue date will coincide with the date that the Articles of Incorporation is granted. 
The securities have been issued in order to be acquired by cualified investors. The Securities will 
be subscribed during the Subscription Period, which will start on the Business Day prior to the 
Disbursement Date (that is to say, 30 November 2005), at 10:00 hours (CET hour) and will end on 
the Disbursement Date (that is to say, 1 December 2005), at 10:00 hours (CET hour). 
The Underwriting and Placement Agents mentioned in section 5.2 of the Registration Document, 
in accordance with the nature of the issue and the customary practices in these markets, may 
distribute the underwritten Securities at their discretion, according to the provisions of the 
Placement Subscription and Underwriting Contract between the Sociedad Gestora and the 
Underwriting and Placement Agents, in all events endeavouring to ensure that no discriminatory 
treatment is given to orders of similar characteristics, notwithstanding which BSIL may give 
priority to the orders from its clients as it deems fit, albeit always taking into consideration the 
instructions received from the other Underwriting and Placement Agents. 
The Bonds will be disbursed on 1 December 2005 (“ Disbursement Date”) at the price of 100% 
of the nominal unit value, except for series A2, which will be an amount between 104.1% and 
106%, as stipulated in section 4.2. supra of this Securities Note. 
Investors to whom the Securities have been allotted must pay the Underwriting and Placement 
Agents, before 10:00 hours (CET time), of the Disbursement Date, for value that same day, the 
issue price of each Security allotted thereto.  
The subscription commitments entered into by each Underwriting and Placement Agent will be 
disbursed before 11:00 hours (CET time), of the Disbursement Date, by means of each 
Underwriting and Placement Agent paying the amount it owes in this respect into the account 
opened by the Paying Agent in the name of the Fund, for value that same day. 
4.14. Restrictions on the free transferability of the securities. 
The Securities are freely transferable and can be transmitted through any legally permissible 
means. Registration of the transfer to the purchaser in the accounting register will have the same 
effects as the trading of shares, and from that moment onwards the transfer can be relied upon as 
against third parties.

5. ADMISSION TO TRADING AND DEALING ARRANGEMENTS 
5.1. 
Market where the securities will be traded 
The Sociedad Gestora, for and on behalf of the Fund, will apply to have the Issue admitted to 
official trading, once the Disbursement has taken place, on the AIAF Fixed Income Market so that 
the Bonds can be traded no later than one (1) month after the Disbursement Date. 
If the Sociedad Gestora fails to have the Securities admitted to trading in the aforementioned time 
frame, it will notify the CNMV accordingly and publish, in a nationwide newspaper, both the 
reasons for such failure and the new date on which the issued Securities are scheduled to be 
admitted to trading, without prejudice to the possibility for the Sociedad Gestora to be held 
contractually liable if the failure is attributable to it. 
The Sociedad Gestora, for and on behalf of the Fund, will request the inclusion of the Securities in 
the accounting register managed by IBERCLEAR, so that their clearing and settlement is effected 
in accordance with the operating rules applicable to securities quoted in the AIAF Fixed Income 
Market established, or to be approved in the future by IBERCLEAR. 
The Sociedad Gestora, for and on behalf of the Fund, hereby declares that it knows the 
requirements and conditions necessary for listing, quotation and delisting of securities in the AIAF 
Fixed Income Market according to the applicable laws and the requirements of its ruling body and 
agrees to comply with the same. 
The Sociedad Gestora, for and on behalf of the Fund, will also request the inclusion of this Issue in 
the accounting register managed by EUROCLEAR and CLEARSTREAM. 
5.2. 
Paying Agent and depository agents 
The payment of interest and principal for the Securities Issue referred to in this Securities Note 
will be handled by SCH, located for these purposes in purposes in Santander (Spain), at Paseo de 
Pereda, 9 - 12, which has the resources to carry out this function. 
The interest of the Securities will be paid on each of the Payment dates, in accordance with the 
terms and conditions set forth in section 4.8 of this Securities Note. 
The Sociedad Gestora, on behalf of and for the account of the Fund, will enter into a Financial 
Services Contract with SCH for the financial servicing of the Securities issued by the Fund 
(hereinafter, “Financial Services Contract”).  
The obligations to be assumed by SCH as paying agent in this Financial Services Contract are as 
summarised below:  
(i) 
On the Disbursement Date, pay to each of the Underwriting and Placement Agents 
the amount of the underwriting and distribution fee owing to each of them. 
(ii) 
On each Payment Date, make the payments to the Security holders and, where 
applicable, to the other entities to which such payments must be made, after 
receiving appropriate instructions from the Sociedad Gestora. 
(iii) 
On each Fixing Date, notify the Sociedad Gestora of the Reference Interest Rate that 
will serve as the basis for calculating the Nominal Interest Rate applicable to each 
Series of the Bonds for each pertinent Interest Accrual Period. 
Furthermore, SCH will act as the custodian of the Multiple Certificates and of the Treasury 
Account, the Collection Account and the Liquidity Line Sinking Account.

Certificates), provided that this is permitted under current law and, if and when necessary, the

must be serious and be liable to harm the interests of the Security holders in the opinion of the 
Rating Agencies. The substitution will be reported to the CNMV, the Rating Agencies and the 
Sellers.

risk of the Paying Agent, which is currently rated as A-1 by S&P and as F1+ by Fitch, are

Series and to the NAS-IO Securities by the Rating Agencies, and after notifying the latter, will put 
into practice, on account of the Fund, one of the options that are described below and are 
necessary, to permit an appropriate level of collateralisation to be maintained with respect to the 
commitments derived from the duties as depository of the Participations and Certificates, paying 
agent, and maintenance of the Treasury Account, the Collection Account and the Liquidity Line 
Sinking Account: 
(a) 
Secure similar guarantees or commitments from one or several credit institutions 
with an S&P rating of no less than A-1, and with a Fitch rating of no less than F1, 
that guarantees the commitments accepted by the Paying Agent;  
(b) 
Substitute the Paying Agent with an entity that has an S&P rating of no less than A-
1, and a Fitch rating of no less than F1. This new entity will perform the Paying 
Agent's duties in the same terms and conditions. 
Furthermore, the Paying Agent will be entitled to terminate the Financial Services Contract by 
giving the Sociedad Gestora at least two (2) months' notice, in accordance with the terms set forth 
in the Financial Services Contract, and provided that (i) another entity of similar financial

The S&P rating is based on the quality of the Participations and the Certificates pooled in the

Issue.

payments or repaying all of the principal of the Participations and the Certificates. The S&P rating 
does not in any way assess the level of return received by investors. 
To perform its analysis, S&P has relied on the statements made by the entities participating in the 
transaction, by their auditors and lawyers, and by other experts, about the accuracy and 
completeness of the information that it has been given in relation to the rating and the subsequent 
monitoring. 
The rating assigned by S&P upon the creation of the Fund may be revised, suspended or 
withdrawn, depending on any information that comes to its notice, or on the non-availability of 
information, or for any other reason. The ratings assigned by Fitch measure the capacity of the 
Fund to timely pay interest on each scheduled Payment Date and repay the principal throughout 
the transaction and, in any event, before the Legal Maturity Date, in accordance with the terms and 
conditions stipulated for the Securities in the Prospectus and in the Articles of Incorporation, 
which allow the delay of payment of interest on the Series B, C and D Bonds under certain 
circumstances. This means that interest might not be received in respect of these Bonds during a 
certain period of time if the delay trigger is reached, with such circumstance not being considered 
an event of default on payment of the Bonds. The Fitch rating of the NAS-IO Security does not 
constitute an assessment of the risk of the Mortgagors making advance payments. 
The ratings assigned by Fitch are based on the documents and information supplied by the issuer, 
and its experts and agents, and are subject to the reception of the final documents. Fitch does not 
audit, verify or check the truth, precision or accuracy of such information. 
Ratings may be changed, qualified, suspended, placed on Rating Watch or withdrawn as a result of 
changes in, additions to, accuracy of, unavailability of or inadequacy of information or for any 
reason Fitch Ratings deems sufficient.

each with a unit face value of one hundred thousand (100,000.00) euros. The amount of the NAS-
IO Securities issue will vary between THREE MILLION NINE HUNDRED AND SEVENTY 
SEVEN THOUSAND (3,977,000) EUROS and FIVE MILLION EIGHT HUNDRED AND 
TWENTY THOUSAND (5,820,000) EUROS, and will consist of NINE HUNDRED AND

2.1. 
Confirmation that the securitised assets have the capacity to produce the funds 
payable on the securities 
In accordance with the information supplied by the Sellers, verified by the Lead Managers, the 
Rating Agencies and the Sociedad Gestora, the Participations and the Certificates to be issued and 
which will be backed by the Mortgage Loans, are of characteristics (amount, term, interest rate, 
mortgage guarantees, etc.) that demonstrate the capacity to produce funds to make the payment 
owed and payable on the Securities, without prejudice to payments to the Securities by the Fund 
having to be made in accordance with the Payment Priority Order and with the subordination 
existing among the different Series.  
However, in order to consolidate its financial structure and procure the largest possible coverage 
for the risks inherent to the issue, the Sociedad Gestora, on behalf of the Fund, will proceed on the 
same date as on which it executes grants the Articles of Incorporation, to formalize the contracts 
and carry out the actions that are stipulated in section 3.4. of this Additional Building Block.

The Participations and the Certificates will be issued by CAJA CASTILLA LA MANCHA,

property valued by a valuation company, and granted pursuant to Spanish law (the “Mortgage 
Loans”).  
The Mortgage Loans will be transferred by the Sellers to the Fund by issuing Participations and 
Certificates in accordance with the individual characteristics of each Mortgage Loan.

Fund will be withdrawn from the loans in the portfolio audited as at 25 October 2005, which

Ernst & Young, whose details are included in section 5.2. of the Registration Document, has 
produced an audit report for the Sociedad Gestora regarding the issue of Participations and 
Certificates for their pooling in the Fund, in order to comply with the provisions of article 5 of 
Royal Decree 926/1998 (the “Audit Report”).  
This Audit Report addresses a series of quantitative and qualitative attributes of the loans, in 
particular: purpose of the loans, identification of the borrowers, date signed, maturity date, 
reference interest rate, current interest rate, interest rate differential, initial amount of the loans, 
current balance of the loans, payment arrears, appraised value, current LTV ratio, address of the 
mortgaged property, mortgage security, material damage insurance and transferability of the loans.
