Termination of the Derivative Contracts 
The early termination of the Derivative Contracts, should it occur, will not, per se, 
constitute sufficient cause for the early termination of the Fund nor for the Early 
Liquidation thereof, unless in combination with other events or circumstances relating to 
the net worth of the Fund, a substantial or permanent change occurs in its financial 
equilibrium. 
The Derivative Contracts will expire on the earlier of (i) the Legal Maturity Date of the 
Fund and (ii) the Date of the Dissolution of the Fund, in accordance with the provisions 
set forth in section 4.4 of the Registration Document. 
The non-confirmation before the start of the Subscription Period of one of the provisional 
ratings assigned to the Bonds by the Rating Agencies will be construed as grounds for 
termination of the Derivative Contracts. 
The Derivative Contracts will also be terminated in the event of the occurrence, before the 
start of the Subscription Period, an event that could not be foreseen or that, despite being 
foreseeable, could not be avoided and makes it impossible to perform the Fund's 
Contracts pursuant to the provisions of section 1,105 of the Civil Code. 
Rating change events 
In the event that the rating of the unsecured and non-subordinated short-term debt of 
Party A (or of its successor) or of the Guarantor of Party A (or of its successor) is 
downgraded, at any time throughout the lifetime of the Securities, to below F1 on the 
Fitch scale or A-1 on the S&P scale, or the rating of the unsecured and non-subordinated 
long-term debt of Party A (or of its successor) or of the Guarantor of Party A (or of its 
successor) is downgraded below A on the Fitch scale (“Rating Event”), Party A will be 
under the obligation, assuming its cost, within a maximum of thirty (30) days of such 
Rating Event occurring, to: 
(i) 
find another entity with a minimum unsecured and non-subordinated short-term debt 
rating of F1, on the Fitch scale and of A-1, on the S&P scale and unsecured and non-
subordinated long-term debt rating of A, on the Fitch scale, that is deemed satisfactory by 
the Sociedad Gestora (which would grant its consent, if the terms and conditions of the 
security maintain the rating of the Securities, or would reestablish the rating of the 
Securities to the level that they had been assigned prior to a Rating Event occurring); or 
(ii) assign its contractual position in the Derivative Contracts to another entity with a 
minimum unsecured and non-subordinated short-term debt rating of F1, on the Fitch scale 
and of A-1, on the S&P scale, and a minimum unsecured and non-subordinated long-term 
debt rating of A on the Fitch scale; or 
(iii) sign the collateral agreement “ISDA Credit Support Annex” (attached to the 
“ISDA” Framework Agreement) within thirty (30) days of the occurrence of the Rating 
Event to guarantee the obligations undertaken in the said framework agreement, which 
must enter into force from the date of notice delivered in accordance with the provisions 
thereof (which must not exceed thirty (30) days from the date of the Rating Event). 
If the conditions of either of paragraphs (i) or (ii) supra  are met at any time, the collateral 
(or their equivalents, where applicable) furnished by Party A in accordance with the

3.7. 
Administrator, Calculation Agent or equivalent 
CAJA CASTILLA LA MANCHA, CREDIFIMO and BANKPIME are acting as the Sellers and 
administrators of the respective Mortgage Loans, and a summary of their obligations and 
responsibilities in such capacity is given below. 
The Sociedad Gestora will be responsible for making the calculations and for performing the 
actions set forth in the Articles of Incorporation and in this Prospectus and in the different Fund 
transaction contracts that are listed in this Prospectus. 
3.7.1. 
Servicing and custody of the Mortgage Loans and deposit of the Participations and 
the Certificates 
Pursuant to the provisions of article 61.3 of Royal Decree 685/1982, and of section 2.b) of 
Article 2 of Royal Decree 926/1998, each Seller will give an undertaking, in the draft 
Articles of Incorporation, to safeguard and service the Mortgage Loans securing the 
Participations and Certificates that it has issued, and will take any action necessary to 
ensure the validity and success of such Mortgage Loans. In any case, the Sociedad 
Gestora, on behalf of the Fund, will be entitled to exercise every right conferred upon the 
owners of participations and certificates under article 66 of Royal Decree 685/1982, in the 
event of a breach arising from non-payment by the Mortgagors. 
Each Seller will be responsible for paying all direct and indirect taxes, levies or expenses 
accrued or incurred by the Seller or that it is obliged to pay as a result of its servicing of 
the corresponding Mortgage Loans, notwithstanding the Seller’s right to be reimbursed 
such taxes, levies and expenses by the borrowers or the Fund, as the case may be.  
General commitments of Sellers as administrators of the Mortgage Loans 
Each Seller will give the Sociedad Gestora and the Fund an undertaking, in the Articles of 
Incorporation of the Fund, and with respect to the Mortgage Loans it services, that it will: 
(i) 
Take any action necessary to ensure the validity and success of the Mortgage Loans, 
in or out of Court, in the conditions established in the following section. 
(ii) Take any action necessary to keep and enforce the collateral and obligations 
deriving from the Mortgage Loans. 
(iii) Take into account the interests of the Security holders in its relationships with the 
borrowers and in exercising any discretional right derived from the performance of 
the services set forth in the Articles of Incorporation and the Prospectus. 
(iv) Comply with all reasonable instructions of the Sociedad Gestora, given in 
accordance with the provisions of the Articles of Incorporation and the Prospectus. 
(v) Take any action necessary to request and keep in full force and effect any licenses, 
approvals, authorizations, and consents that may be necessary or appropriate relating 
to the performance of its services. 
(vi) Have sufficient personnel and equipment to comply with all its obligations.

Mortgage Loan servicing services 
1. 
Custody and collection management 
In servicing the Mortgage Loans, each Seller will devote the same time and attention 
thereto, and will exercise the same level of skill, care and diligence in their servicing as it 
would devote and exercise in servicing non-transferred mortgage loans and, in any case, it 
will exercise a reasonable level of skill, care and diligence in rendering its services. 
Each Seller will remain subject to the criteria established under Annex 7 of the Articles of 
Incorporation for the servicing of the Mortgage Loans, although it may modify such 
criteria provided that such modifications do not impair the servicing of the Mortgage 
Loans, are reported to the Sociedad Gestora and are not, in any way, detrimental to the 
rating assigned to the Securities by the Rating Agencies and, additionally, provided that it 
is subject to the negotiation limits specified in number 6 of this section. 
Specifically, each Seller will keep every notarial deed, document and file relating to the 
Mortgage Loans it services, and to any other right accessory to such Mortgage Loans, as 
well as any pertinent documents relating thereto, under safe custody, and will not 
relinquish the possession, custody or control of the Mortgage Loans without the prior 
written consent of the Sociedad Gestora, on behalf of the Fund, unless such 
relinquishment is (i) in favour of an appointed subcontractor or delegate, providing that 
this is permitted by the current regulations; or (ii) to allow the Seller to bring proceedings 
for the foreclosure of a Mortgage Loan, as administrator of the loans; 
Each Seller, as administrator of the Loans, will collect every amount due and payable 
under the Mortgage Loans or any right accessory to them and will make every efforts to 
ensure the collection of all payments to be made by the borrowers or by other persons, 
under the Mortgage Loans or any other right accessory to them, in accordance with the 
terms and conditions of such Mortgage Loans and on the corresponding date.   
In the event of discrepancies between any Seller and the Sociedad Gestora regarding the 
amount such Seller must deliver the Fund on each Calculation Date, regarding both the 
collected amount as well as the Technical Advance, both parties will make every effort to 
settle such discrepancies. However, should no agreement be reached before the 
Calculation Date, the Seller will provisionally deliver the Fund the amount established by

2. 
Actions against the Mortgagors 
In the event of delay in the payments to which Mortgagors are bound under the 
transferred Mortgage Loans, each Seller, as administrator of such Mortgage Loans, will 
take the actions described in Annex 7 of the Articles of Incorporation, adopting the 
measures that a reasonably prudent mortgagee conducting financing transactions in Spain 
would take, providing that the exercise of such discretional rights does not affect the Fund 
management, or the rating assigned to the Securities.  
In any case, and if the Mortgagor fails to pay the Mortgage Loans securing the issuance of 
the Participations and Certificates pooled in the Fund, the Sociedad Gestora, on behalf of 
the Fund, as their holder, will be entitled to exercise all the rights set forth in Article 66 of 
Royal Decree 685/1982.  
In the event of a joinder situation as provided under Article 66, section b), of Royal 
Decree 685/1982, the Seller in question will be entitled to award in payment and the 
auction proceeds will be distributed as stated in the aforementioned article. 
In the event that any of the situations described in Article 66, sections c) and d), of Royal 
Decree 685/1982 arises and, as a result thereof, the Sociedad Gestora, on behalf of the 
Fund, subrogates such Seller in the proceedings brought by the latter, or brings 
foreclosure proceedings, the Sociedad Gestora will sell the allocated real property in the 
shortest possible term under market conditions. The corresponding Seller will hold a right 
of first refusal for the acquisition of that real property securing as collateral the Mortgage 
Loans it services, and allocated to the Fund, within the following ten (10) Business Days 
from the date in which such Seller is notified by the Sociedad Gestora, by satisfactory 
means, of the intention to transfer the real property. The right of first refusal will imply 
that the pertinent Seller can acquire the real property under the same terms and conditions 
as offered to the Sociedad Gestora. 
All the actions mentioned in this section regarding the Participations and Certificates will 
be performed in accordance with the terms established in Book III, Title IV of the Ley de 
Enjuiciamiento Civil  (Law 1/2000). 
3. 
Actions against the Sellers 
The Sociedad Gestora, on behalf of and for the account of the Fund, will be entitled to 
take enforcement proceedings against the Sellers to collect any past due principal and 
interest of the Mortgage Loans, if the reason for the non-payment of such items is not the 
result of non-payment by the Mortgagors. 
Furthermore, should any Seller be in breach of the obligations described in the previous 
section, the Fund, through the Sociedad Gestora, will be entitled to bring a declaratory 
action against such Seller for breaching its obligations in relation to the Mortgage Loans, 
proceeding pursuant to the provisions of the Ley de Enjuiciamiento Civil. 
Upon termination of the Mortgage Loans, the Fund, through its Sociedad Gestora, will 
remain be entitled to take action against the Sellers until they have complied with their 
obligations.

5. 
Substitution of the Sellers as the Mortgage Loan administrators 
Should the Sociedad Gestora find that any Seller is in breach of the obligations stipulated 
in this section as administrator of the respective Mortgage Loans, or find about any events 
that, in the opinion of the Sociedad Gestora, imply a detriment or risk for the financial 
structure of the Fund or the rights and interests of Security holders, the Sociedad Gestora 
may, if permitted under the current legal framework, (i) substitute the Seller in question 
as administrator of the Mortgage Loans or (ii) demand that the Seller in question 
subcontract or delegate the performance of such obligations to or on a person who, in the 
opinion of the Sociedad Gestora, is suitably qualified technically to perform such duties. 
The Sociedad Gestora will consider any proposals made by the Seller in question 
regarding the appointment of its substitute. The Seller will be bound to execute such 
subcontract or delegation. 
Furthermore, if a corporate, legal or court decision is made or issued for the dissolution, 
winding-up or receivership of any Seller, or any Seller files a petition to be declared 
bankrupt, or a Court allows a request filed by a third party, the Sociedad Gestora will 
substitute the pertinent Seller as administrator of the Mortgage Loans, providing that this 
is permitted by the applicable Law. 
If permitted by the applicable Law, the new administrator of the Mortgage Loans will, 
where applicable, be appointed by the Sociedad Gestora, after consulting the competent 
administrative authorities, in order to avoid any detriment to the rating assigned to the 
Securities by the Ratings Agencies, who will be notified of such appointment. The 
Sociedad Gestora may agree the amount to be paid with the new administrator, at the 
expense of the Fund and, specifically, payable from the individual account of the Seller in 
question, as it deems appropriate. Such amount will be deemed an extraordinary expense 
and will be paid pursuant to the Payment Priority Order.  
If permitted by the applicable Law, any Seller may request to be substituted in servicing 
the Mortgage Loans; all expenses incurred in such substitution will be at the Seller’s 
expense. The Sociedad Gestora will authorize such substitution, provided that the 
requesting Seller has found an entity to substitute it in its servicing capacity, and such 
substitution is not detrimental to the rating assigned to the Securities by the Rating 
Agencies, who will be notified of such appointment. 
In the event of substitution, the substituted Seller will supply the new administrator with 
the documents necessary to provides the services in question.

6. 
Modifications to the Mortgage Loans 
Pursuant to article 25 of Royal Decree 685/1982, dated 17 March, without the consent of 
the Sociedad Gestora and with respect to the respective Mortgage Loans that they service, 
none of the Sellers will voluntarily cancel the mortgages on any grounds other than the 
payment of the Mortgage Loans, waive or settle such mortgages, substitute the Mortgage 
Loans through novation, write them off in full or part or defer them nor, in general, take 
any step that diminishes the range, legal efficiency or economic value of the mortgage or 
the Mortgage Loans , with the exception of the authorized modifications mentioned in the 
next paragraph. 
Each Seller, as administrator of its respective Mortgage Loans, will be authorized, from 
the Date of Incorporation and with respect to such Mortgage Loans, provided that the 
rating assigned to the Securities issued by the Fund is not impaired in any way, the 
payments to be made to the Fund are not adversely affected, and it notifies the Sociedad 
Gestora which, in turn, will notify the Rating Agencies, to: 
(i) 
Allow the subrogation of the Mortgage Loan contracts, solely in the event that the 
characteristics of the new Mortgagor are similar to the characteristics of the previous 
Mortgagor, and that such characteristics conform to the policy set forth in the 
respective Seller’s Internal Memo on Granting of Mortgage Loans. 
(ii) Agree with the Mortgagors to modify the interest rate and final maturity of the 
Mortgage Loans, provided that the terms and conditions set forth in sections 7 and 8 
infra are met. 
7. 
Interest rate modifications 
Pursuant to the provisions of the Articles of Incorporation and this Prospectus, if any 
Seller agrees to modify the interest of any Mortgage Loan that it services and, 
consequently, to modify the corresponding Participation or Certificate, the Fund will still 
be entitled to all the ordinary interest accrued by the Mortgage Loan.  
Each Seller may negotiate a lowering of the interest rate differential applicable to the 
Mortgage Loans underlying the issue of Participations and Certificates, without regard to 
its reference rate, provided that the new weighed average differential of the Participations 
and Certificates it has issued does not imply a reduction or more than 20% in the weighed 
average differential of the Participations and Certificates it has issued, on the Date of 
Incorporation. 
For these purposes, any modifications that lower or raise the interest rate differential 
applicable to the Mortgage Loans will not be construed as novations or renegotiations, if 
such variations are previously agreed upon under the Mortgage Loans notarial deeds.  
8. 
Modifications to final maturity of the loans 
Pursuant to the provisions of the Articles of Incorporation and this Prospectus, each Seller 
may modify the final maturity date of the Mortgage Loans it services and underlying the 
Participations and Certificates they issue, provided that the following conditions are met: 
(i) 
The frequency of the Mortgage Loan principal repayment instalments remains 
unchanged or is reduced, and the repayment system is maintained. 
(ii) The new final maturity date of the loan does not fall after 10 June 2037.

(iii) During the last six months prior to the time that the term is to be modified, all the

(vi) The amount of the initial balance of the Participations and Certificates whose period

Participations and Certificates of that Seller pooled in the Fund. 
Under no circumstances may the Seller, as administrator of the Mortgage Loans, decide to 
modify the period of maturity of a Mortgage Loan without a request from the Mortgagor. 
The administrator will always considers the Fund’s interests in making any such 
modification. 
The Sociedad Gestora, for and on behalf of the Fund, may cancel or suspend each Seller’s 
permission to modify the period of maturity, at any time throughout the life of the Fund. 
The modification of a Mortgage Loan will not result in such Loan ceasing to conform to 
the characteristics set forth in section 2.2.8.3. of this Additional Building Block. 
In the event of renegotiation of the interest rate of any Mortgage Loan, or its final 
maturity, the Seller in question, as administrator of such Mortgage Loan, will 
immediately notify the Sociedad Gestora of the renegotiated terms and conditions, 
notwithstanding the specific interest rate renegotiation provisions set forth in this section 
of the Prospectus.  
Deposit of the Participations and the Certificates 
The Multiple Securities that represent the Participations and the Certificates issued by the 
Sellers will be deposited with the Paying Agent, who will act as the depository thereof.  
3.7.2. 
Description of the duties and responsibilities undertaken by the Sociedad Gestora 
regarding the management and legal representation of the Fund and Security 
holders 
1. 
Duties and responsibilities of the Sociedad Gestora 
The Fund will be incorporated by TITULIZACIÓN DE ACTIVOS, S.G.F.T., S.A. as the 
Sociedad Gestora authorised for such purposes and, consequently, to act as the manager 
and legal representative of the Fund, pursuant to the provisions of Royal Decree 
926/1998. 
As the manager of third party funds, the Sociedad Gestora is also responsible for 
representing and safeguarding the interests of the Security holders. 
The Security holders will have no recourse against the Sociedad Gestora, other than from 
non-performance of its duties or non-compliance with the provisions of the Articles of 
Incorporation, of this Prospectus and the applicable laws and regulations.

Merely by way of illustration, and notwithstanding other actions stipulated in the Articles 
of Incorporation and this Prospectus, the duties of the Sociedad Gestora will be as 
follows: 
(i) 
Check that the amount of the revenues actually received by the Fund matches the 
revenues that the Fund should have received, in accordance with the provisions of the 
different contracts from which such revenues derive. Should it be necessary, the Sociedad 
Gestora will take any action, either in court or out of court, necessary or appropriate to 
protect the rights of the Fund and Security holders. 
(ii) 
Apply the Fund’s revenues to the payment of the Fund’s obligations, as provided 
in the Articles of Incorporation and this Prospectus. 
(iii) 
Extend the term or modify the contracts it has entered into on behalf of the Fund in 
order to allow the Fund to operate in the terms stipulated in the Articles of Incorporation, 
this Prospectus and the laws applicable from time to time.  
(iv) 
Substitute each person rendering services to the Fund, under the terms established 
in the Articles of Incorporation and this Prospectus, provided that such substitution is 
permitted by the laws applicable from time to time, is authorized by the competent 
authorities, if necessary, the Rating Agencies are notified and such action is not 
detrimental to the interests of the Security holders. In particular, in the event that any 
Seller is in breach of its obligations as the administrator of its respective Mortgage Loans, 
the Sociedad Gestora will take any steps necessary to ensure the proper servicing of the 
Mortgage Loans. 
(v) 
Issue appropriate instructions to the Payment Agent in relation to the Treasury 
Account, the Collection Account, the Liquidity Line Sinking Account and, to the Rated 
Sellers, if the Reinvestment Accounts are opened and, where applicable, to the entity 
where the Surplus Treasury Account is opened, in relation to such account.  
(vi) 
Issue appropriate instructions to the Payment Agent in relation to payments to be 
made to the Security holders and, were applicable, to other entities in charge of making 
payments. 
(vii) 
Where applicable, calculate and make the Initial Expenses Loan principal and 
interest payments. 
(viii) Calculate and make the Liquidity Line sinking payments. 
(ix) 
Calculate and make the Fund payments under the Derivative Contracts. 
(x) 
Appoint and replace the auditor, where applicable, with the prior approval of the 
CNMV, where necessary. 
(xi) 
Produce and submit to the competent agencies any documents and information that 
must be submitted under current regulations, to the CNMV, and produce and disclose to 
the Security holders any information that is legally required. 
(xii) 
Make appropriate decisions relating to the liquidation of the Fund, including the 
decision to proceed with the early liquidation of the Fund, pursuant to the provisions of 
the Articles of incorporation and this Prospectus. 
(xiii) Determine the rate of interest applicable to Series of Bonds in each Interest 
Accrual Period.

2. 
Resignation and substitution of the Sociedad Gestora. 
The resignation and substitution of the Sociedad Gestora will be governed by Royal 
Decree 926/1998 or the laws in force from time to time. Be that as it may, the Sociedad 
Gestora will be substituted in accordance with the procedure described below, provided 
that such procedure is not in conflict with the regulatory provisions established for such 
purposes:  
1. 
The Sociedad Gestora may resign from such duties whenever it deems such 
resignation appropriate and voluntarily ask to be substituted by submitting a written 
request to the CNMV. The request must enclose a document from the new Sociedad 
Gestora, which must be properly authorized and registered in the Special Registers of the 
CNMV, in which the new Sociedad Gestora states that it is willing to accept such duties 
and seeks appropriate authorization. The resignation of the Sociedad Gestora and the 
appointment of a new company as the Sociedad Gestora of the Fund must be approved by 
the CNMV. Under no circumstances will the Sociedad Gestora resign from its duties until 
all the requirements and formalities have been completed and its substitute can take over 
its duties with respect to the Fund. Furthermore, the Sociedad Gestora will not be entitled 
to resign from its duties if such substitution leads to the downgrading of the rating 
assigned to the Securities by the Rating Agencies. Any expenses incurred in such 
substitution will be for the account of the Sociedad Gestora or, where applicable, of the 
new Sociedad Gestora. 
2. 
The Sociedad Gestora will be substituted in the event of the occurrence, in the 
Sociedad Gestora, of any of the causes for dissolution set forth in article 260, number 1, 
of the Ley de Sociedades Anónimas (Spanish Corporations Act). The Sociedad Gestora 
will report the occurrence of any such cause to the CNMV and the Rating Agencies. In 
this event, the Sociedad Gestora will be bound to comply with the provisions of number 1 
above, before its dissolution. 
3. 
In the event that the Sociedad Gestora is declared bankrupt or its authorization is 
withdrawn, it will proceed to appoint a substitute Sociedad Gestora. The substitution must 
take place within four (4) months of the date on which the event giving rise to such 
substitution occurs. Should the Sociedad Gestora fail to find another Sociedad Gestora 
willing to take over the administration and representation of the Fund or the CNMV 
consider that the proposal is not suitable and may result in the rating of the Securities 
being downgraded, the Fund will be liquidated in advance and the Bonds redeemed, four 
(4) months after the event giving rise to the substitution has occurred. 
4. 
The substitution of the Sociedad Gestora and the appointment of a new Sociedad 
Gestora, approved by the CNMV as stipulated in the preceding paragraphs, must be 
accepted by the Rating Agencies, and published in the AIAF Fixed Income Market Daily 
Bulletin. The Sociedad Gestora undertakes to grant any necessary private and public 
documents for its substitution by another Sociedad Gestora, pursuant to the provisions of 
the previous paragraphs. The substitute sociedad gestora must be subrogated to the rights 
and obligations of the Sociedad Gestora relating to this Prospectus and the Articles of 
Incorporation. Furthermore, the Sociedad Gestora will hand over to the new Sociedad 
Gestora any accounting or computer documents and records relating to the Fund in its 
possession.

3. 
Remuneration of the Sociedad Gestora for performing its duties. 
On each Payment Date, the Sociedad Gestora will receive as remuneration for its services, 
a quarterly management fee, equal, except for the first Payment Date, to a quarter of 
0.03% of the Outstanding Nominal Balance of the Participations and Certificates on the 
previous Payment Date. Such fee will be construed as a gross fee, insofar as it includes 
any direct or indirect tax or withholding that may be levied on it. The fee on each 
Payment Date will not be lower than a quarter of 0.02% of the initial balance of the 
Participations and Certificates issued by each Seller and will not exceed 140,000 Euros. 
This amounts will be updated at the beginning of each calendar year (starting in 2006), in 
accordance with the General Consumer Price Index as published by Spain’s National 
Statistical Institute (“Instituto Nacional de Estadística”) or such body as may substitute it. 
On the first Payment Date, the management fee will be adjusted by the number of days 
elapsed since the Disbursement Date.

AIAF bulletin, or in such other as may replace it or with similar characteristics,

general or business and financial nature, such notification being deemed 
effective on the date of the abovementioned publication, which may fall on any 
day of the year, whether a Business or Non-Business Day (as stipulated in this 
Prospectus). 
As an exception, the liquidation of the Fund may be carried out by means of 
publication in a widely circulated newspaper in Spain of either a general or 
economic and financial nature, with such notification being considered as 
effective on the date of the abovementioned publication, which may fall on any 
day of the year, whether a Business or Non-Business Day (according to this 
Prospectus).
